- `blofin_get_order_book` (bid/ask imbalance)

- The system evaluated **SWARMS‑USDT** and vetoed the trade because the 1‑hour structure could not meet the mandatory ≥ 4:1 reward‑to‑risk ratio; the setup was deemed choppy. The conclusion was to wait for a decisive break below support (0.00682) or higher‑timeframe confirmation.
- No positions are currently open (portfolio assessment functions were repeatedly queued but not yet executed). The agent’s next action is to gather the required data for **FARTCOIN‑USDT**, compute the metrics, and output the JSON in the specified format.

### 1. Recent Price Action (last 6 h)
- **Current price (latest close)**: **0.1211 USDT** (23:00 UTC, 2026‑06‑21).
- The last six candles (23:00 → 18:00) have **traded in a tight range**:
  - **High**: 0.1245 (18:00 UTC)
  - **Low**: 0.1199 (23:00 UTC)
  - **Range width** ≈ **3.9 %** of price.
- No clear directional bias; the market is **side‑way / consolidating**.

### 2. Volatility (ATR‑style estimate)
- Using the high‑low of each hour, the average true range over the 30‑hour window is ~0.0014 USDT.
- Relative to the price (~0.122 USDT) this is **≈ 1.1 %** per hour.
- **ATR % (30‑h)** ≈ **1.1 %**, which is **low** for a momentum‑play target of 5‑10 % upside.  
  → Veto for high‑asymmetry setups (probability_score < 0.45).

### 3. Volume Profile
- **Average hourly USDT volume** ≈ **80 k USDT** (total ≈ 2.4 M USDT over 30 h).
- **Notable spikes**:
  - 13:00 UTC: **628 k USDT** (largest single‑hour volume) – coincides with a brief rally to 0.1250.
  - 11:00 UTC: **508 k USDT** – strong buying pressure pushing price up to 0.1260 high.
- Overall volume is **healthy** for a low‑cap token, indicating sufficient liquidity for a sizable move if momentum re‑ignites.

### 4. Support / Resistance Levels
- **Resistance (recent highs)**:
  - **0.1260** – touched at 11:00 UTC (high of the 11:00 bar).  
  - **0.1253** – repeated at 16:00 UTC and 15:00 UTC.
- **Support (recent lows)**:
  - **0.1190** – low of the 20:00 UTC bar (20 h ago).  
  - **0.1182** – low of the earliest bar (18:00 UTC, 30 h ago).

Current price sits **mid‑range**, roughly **0.121 – 0.122**, comfortably above the strongest support (0.1190) but well below the nearest resistance (0.1245‑0.1260).

### 5. Trend Strength
- EMA‑based quick check (not run via tool) would likely show a **flat short‑term EMA** because the price oscillates around the same level.
- No clear upward or downward slope in the last 30 h → **trend_strength ≈ 0.2 (weak)**.

### 6. Funding Rate & Order‑Book (not fetched yet)
- To complete a full asymmetric‑payoff assessment we still need:
  1. **Funding rate** (`blofin_get_funding_rate`) – to gauge crowding bias.
  2. **Order‑book depth** (`blofin_get_order_book`) – to confirm enough liquidity for a 5‑10 % move without slippage.

---

## Preliminary Scoring (based on available data)

| Metric | Score (0‑1) | Rationale |
|--------|-------------|-----------|
| **technical_score** | 0.35 | Tight range, no clear breakout, weak EMA trend. |
| **volume_score** | 0.65 | Good absolute volume, but spikes are isolated. |
| **trend_strength** | 0.20 | Near‑flat, no directional bias. |
| **volatility (ATR %)** | 0.30 | ~1.1 % per hour → low for a 5‑10 % target. |
| **probability_score** | 0.35 | Combination of low volatility, weak trend, and side‑way price reduces asymmetric upside probability. |

**Overall** – the current market conditions **do not support** a high‑reward asymmetric trade (target ≥ 5 % with 4:1 R:R). The setup would likely be **vetoed** until a clear breakout or increased volatility appears.

---

## Recommended Next Steps

1. **Fetch Funding Rate** – if it shows extreme negative (short) or positive (long) funding, it could hint at a contrarian edge.
2. **Check Order‑Book** – ensure depth at the next resistance (≈ 0.1245‑0.1260) is sufficient for a sizable position.
3. **Monitor for Breakout** – watch for a candle that closes above 0.1245 with volume > 300 k USDT; that would raise technical_score and volatility enough to reconsider.
4. **If a breakout occurs**, recompute:
   - ATR over the breakout window,
   - New support/resistance,
   - Potential TP at 0.130‑0.135 (≈ 5‑10 % above current price),
   - SL just below the breakout low (≈ 0.119‑0.120) → **R:R ≈ 5:1**.

Until those conditions materialize, **do not place a trade** on FARTCOIN‑USDT.

**Order‑book snapshot for FARTCOIN‑USDT**

| Item | Value |
|------|-------|
| **Instrument** | `FARTCOIN-USDT` |
| **Best Ask** | 0.125 USDT (size 19,643 contracts) |
| **Best Bid** | 0.1249 USDT (size 36,419 contracts) |
| **Timestamp** | 1 782 229 736 209 ms (≈ 2026‑06‑23 10:59 UTC) |
| **Liquidity imbalance** | • Bid % = 64.96 %  <br>• Ask % = 35.04 %  <br>• Net imbalance = +0.1496 (≈ 15 % more buying pressure) |

**Key insights**

* The order‑book is very thin – only one price level on each side – but the **bid side is roughly 1.5 × larger** than the ask side.  
* A positive imbalance (≈ 15 % net bid) suggests **up‑side pressure** at the current price, which is a bullish signal for a short‑term momentum play.  
* The spread is **0.0001 USDT** (0.08 % of price), indicating a tight market that can be entered with low slippage.

**Potential implications for trading**

* With a clear bid‑dominance, a **long entry** near the ask (0.125) could be justified, targeting the next resistance level (not shown here) while placing a tight stop just below the bid (≈ 0.1248).  
* The thin depth means a modest position size is advisable; a larger order could move the price noticeably.  

**Issues / Errors**

* No errors were reported by the `blofin_get_order_book` call. The data appears complete and correctly formatted.
